New Basketball Techniques (7) (No Reproduction Allowed) Original Author Claire Burcky 96

During the game, if a player fails to hold the ball and it slips out of bounds, or if someone dribbling the ball fails to stop immediately and slides out of bounds, or if the ball slips out of bounds due to a careless mistake, it is not only detrimental to the team but also lengthens the opponent's attack, as the opponent gets to throw the ball back in.

The following are some rules: (1) If any part of a player's body touches the outside of the boundary line or the end line, the ball is out of bounds. (2) If any part of the ball touches the boundary line, the floor, or bounces outside the field, the ball is out of bounds. (3) If a player within the boundary line touches the ball and causes it to go out of bounds, the ball is also out of bounds.

After the ball goes out of bounds, the game is restarted by a player from the opposing team that caused the ball to go out of bounds standing outside the boundary line and throwing the ball to a teammate. If the thrower dribbles the ball into the field or touches the ball again after it enters the field without being touched by another player, or if they fail to throw the ball in after five seconds, the referee will whistle and award the ball to the opposing team (the one who originally caused the ball to go out of bounds) to throw it in from outside the boundary line.

If officials are unable to determine which team caused the ball to go out of bounds, the referee may choose two players from the two teams to jump for the ball at a point one yard inside the boundary line, directly at right angles from where the ball went out.

Page 10

Free Talk

If Gandhi Were in China 97

— Jing Ji

The committee to support the League of Nations covenant in this city sent a letter urging Mr. Xiang Laoren to take the post of honorary member; because the letter mentioned imitating Gandhi's non-cooperation movement, Xiang Laoren told me the following:

If Gandhi were in China, how would he save China? The so-called non-cooperation movement would have to change its methods? I will tell you the reasons in two layers; but in the end, it's like the saying: the same old story!

First, the problem of national belief. You must understand that religious power can transform the people into customs and unite the people's hearts. Gandhi is very religious in India; the general Indian people regard him as a devout religious figure: so this kind of personality is enough to call on the people. Think: Ireland also demanded autonomy from England in the same way, and now it has regained autonomy; because most Irish people are Catholic! Gandhi's actions would not attract the same sympathy from Chinese people with weak beliefs; therefore, another method must be devised.

Second, the problem of local customs. Our country has a vast territory and a large population, and the customs of the north and south are different: the northeast is ravaged by Japan, and the southwest's attitude is the same as usual; the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai is fierce, but Japanese goods are thriving in Tianjin. It is very shameful to say: the kneeling and crying groups' weeping and kowtowing, how have the consciences of the unscrupulous merchants awakened: Gandhi must think of another ingenious plan for these numb Chinese people!

If Gandhi were really born in China, and lived to be over ninety years old like me, and understood our people's customs, I hope he would cooperate with me: to correct people's hearts by preaching the Ten Commandments, and to promote local baojia [household registration system] and implement self-government. Luan Cheng's essay on civil administration says that in ancient times, the Three Elders and Se Fu [local officials] were used to ridicule and teach the unworthy elements of their townships and counties; now, if we promote people's autonomy, the unscrupulous merchants will not be able to escape the public judgment of their neighbors and fellow villagers!"

Internal Disaster 98

— Ah Hong

Starting from the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom

The demise of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, its fatal wound was internal disaster. After reading Shi Dakai's poems, one cannot help but sigh! However, this was not accidental: thinking of that group of heroes from the wilderness, they originally started their own business, and what they said about comforting the people and punishing the guilty was just propaganda and a means of calling on the people. Where was it true! Therefore, once they gained power, they indulged in fine wine and women, and fought for power and profit! For the sake of personal grievances, even if it harmed the country and the people, they would not care! They monopolized the power of victory, and if they failed, they would return to being rogues. What was impossible! However, this was eighty years ago, when the world was a one-surname family. The winner is king, and the loser is a bandit, which has nothing to do with the common people. But now it is different: the master is our 400 million people! Even if Cao Cao were reborn, he would say: I am a public servant! I am a pioneer for the people!

However, the internal disaster in our country now is even worse than that of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom! And the foreign troubles are even greater than they were then! Before, the people did not know that they could use their power, but now we have power, but we never use it, which is regrettable!

Compatriots! Don't be willing to be plague gods or Adou [incompetent rulers] again, shrinking your heads, clenching your teeth, and enduring it! Honestly and impolitely exercise your power as masters! Let's immediately issue an urgent decree ordering our public servants:

First, if you still feel that you are our public servants, you should immediately stop the civil war, go to the border, and aim your guns at the enemy!

Second, if you insist on being brave and ruthless against your own people, then please immediately take down your public servant sign and go to the circus, bullfighting arena, or set up your own arena! Feel free to show off your skills and fight for territory! But don't tarnish us by fighting under our banner! Fellow men and women: wake up! If we don't sanction them: they will show off their power until they are satisfied, but they cannot share the pain of being slaves to a conquered nation for you!

Bare-Legged Women 99

— Qiu Zhaowei

This Era Is Ours

Old Zhang said: "It's getting cold, shouldn't those women walking on the street with their legs bare put on their socks? I said: "No, socks are not worn even in winter. Because even old women's legs may not get frostbite."

"Even their thighs are bare, their buttocks swaying in cheongsams, almost not wearing pants, what is this?"

"But, if there is no considerable healthy beauty and youthful blood color, they would never want to be exposed."

"The most important things for women are their chests, bellies, and buttocks. How to make them develop freely and fully, and how to make them show off, are all important. That is to say, you want natural beauty, posture, and the undulation of curves."

"Is black, yellow, and brown skin also considered beautiful? Isn't that just seducing carnal desire and not wearing pants? If they ran out of a brothel, or are street prostitutes, there's nothing to be surprised about, but these are actually ladies from respectable families and female students! Degeneracy, incredible degeneracy! Our moral culture is on the road to extinction!"

"But, please don't say that. Because it's because of this era! It is said that in the big era, everything is changing, is leaping, it is said that the children of the era are standing at the forefront, showing the lively power of youth, so as women, they are returning to the primitive, free, semi-nude state."

"But I don't know why, I always feel a little worried," said Old Zhang.

Life Scale 100

— Shan Mu Gong

Enjoyment and Happiness Are Inversely Proportional

"This place is so big, there's simply nothing delicious. Tell Secretary Zhao. Urgent telegram to Old Qiu to ask him to buy some water pears in Laiyang and some peaches in Weicheng. Must be delivered by tomorrow morning..."

"...Ah Chun, yesterday's table of dishes was really too unbearable; the chicken was old, and there was too little crab roe: if you don't buy Japanese shark fin, don't you have Western ones either? Today, I'll spend thirty yuan to arrange another feast, it should be authentic, right?..."

"...Chef He is really damned seven times! So few dishes for a table of seven people; the meat slices are cut so thin, and the fish are picked so small, how is that enough to eat? The meal money was paid long ago when school started, I wonder how much he's going to pocket!..."

"...We have simple tea and plain rice for three meals a day, it's really not easy. If we switched to a government job, even with 30% of our monthly salary, we would still be two months in debt. Maybe we wouldn't even have a long gown!..."

"...Running around all day today, although my legs ache and my back is sore, I still made 500 wen. It's not enough for my family to eat a few bowls of white rice, so we can only fill our stomachs with big cakes. If I were to sit at home, it would be hard to say..."

"...Old folks! We've been lying in the fields for two days and two nights, let me stab to death eight Japanese devils. If I could kill a few more, then even if I haven't eaten or drunk for three days, I wouldn't feel anything, but would feel happy..."

The "Big" Gets Tricked 101

— Cao Lifang

Just Because the "Small" Is in Power

This journal published Feng Jun's article "The 'Small' Is in Power" nine issues ago, and after further investigation, I am filled with emotion! Because "the 'small' is in power" has created the bad result of the "big" getting tricked. Now, I will elaborate on some of the examples cited by Feng Jun:

The psychology of us Chinese people, especially, is characterized by the "big." It is almost universally built on the foundation of loving the "small." Just look: the "big" person's most beloved is not his wife, but his "small" wife. But not every "small" wife is able to receive the "big" person's love and reciprocate it with heartfelt affection, without looking elsewhere; the "big" official's usual residence is not his official residence, but his "small" mansion, but the beauties inside the "small" mansion do not necessarily consider the "big" official's financial burden and live a frugal life, in order to reduce his extravagant 金屋式 [referring to the extravagant lifestyle of keeping a mistress]; "the 'small' ones" among the prostitutes possess seductive magic, especially being able to make "big" young masters with huge fortunes spend money like water. Once the money is gone, they will refuse to see guests; "the 'small' ones" with white faces among boyfriends are especially able to move people to pity, especially being able to make "big" family daughters who are obsessed with beauty fall in love at first sight. Once their bodies are defiled, they will be discarded without hesitation; as for the psychology of people who read "small" newspapers, they completely misunderstand reading newspapers as a way to relieve boredom and forget the more important meaning of reading newspapers. As a result, the sales of "big" newspapers are inevitably affected, so that our country's news industry is still lagging behind in the international arena!

Speaking of the country, our "big" China, because the "small" eastern neighbor is "in power," the result of "big" China being "tricked" is that, to this day, the disaster of national subjugation is imminent! Can we still not wake up, but continue to cling to our inherent psychology of loving the "small," feeling that the "small" eastern neighbor is "small" enough to be pitiful, "small" enough to be cute, without thinking of slightly changing its bad nature and fighting to the death with this "small" eastern neighbor, who is our country's enemy and the world's public enemy? (Not paid)

In Pursuit of Happiness with Fellow Travelers (4) 102

— The Master of Happiness

"Oh! Yizhen, you finally came!" He jumped up suddenly, grasped the hand of the person behind him, and asked anxiously: "I don't mind waiting a little longer, but I was just thinking that you agreed to meet me here at four thirty yesterday to talk. You would never break your promise for no reason, so something must have happened. I've been worried sick about you here!"

After saying those words, the young man held the visitor's hand tightly, unwilling to let go, and focused his eyes on her for a good, long look. The visitor was a woman, wearing a fish-white bamboo cloth short jacket, tied with a green crepe short skirt, white long stockings, and black leather shoes. She was an extremely plain female student. Her hair had been cut short, and a neat fringe of short hair covered her forehead, making her look like a young Western girl. A pair of black, shiny, round eyes, a nose like a hanging gallbladder, and naturally rosy cheeks made her look like a truly innocent and lively young girl of sixteen or seventeen. But at this golden age, when she should be happy and lively, she now showed a hint of melancholy for some reason.

He saw all of this – her appearance and expression – very clearly in an instant and couldn't help but ask: "Ya, your complexion is very bad; I guessed correctly, you must have encountered some adversity in your family again. Don't bottle it up, tell me quickly!" The girl lowered her head and slowly replied in a very quiet voice: "Boqin, you guessed right; I, with my extremely lonely and unfortunate destiny, have now encountered an extremely serious turn of events. You know my background very well. I am an orphan with no parents, relying on my uncle to live. I am determined not to rely on them too much, and I am trying my best to get some knowledge and learn some skills, so I can open a path for myself and find an independent occupation. Even when I usually receive some cold looks from my aunt and uncle and suffer some grievances, I think of them as temporary and insignificant hardships that I can avoid sooner or later, so I can put up with them and just get by. But what I am encountering today is not so ordinary and simple! My aunt and uncle insist on carrying out some kind of "qinshang" [interference from relatives] and taking charge of my marriage. My aunt is even worse, a wicked and materialistic woman from the lowest of brothels. She has bewitched my uncle, saying that she is helping him find connections to become an official, and she spends day and night outside socializing with officials' wives. She can't get close to the wealthy, so she hangs out with the adjutants and orderlies of high-ranking military officers.

New News about Long-Term Loans 106

In the silver and money industries, there must be a large number of long-term settlements or new loans every year in March and September. Since the business community adopted the Gregorian calendar in the 18th year of the Republic, it has been changed to April and October. Now that the time for the October event has arrived again, the qianzhuang side has slightly saved long-term settlements in the past few days, with an estimated amount of about 3 million. The amount of long-term debts due is more than 1 million. There are many transfers, and the number of settlements is less than 1 million. As for the price, there is currently no certainty. Roughly speaking, there must be a kind of fixed price announcement when a large number of them are collected. According to silver and money industry news, not many loans were released in the previous session (April), and this time there may be no special impact from the collection.

Autumn Harvest is Abundant, Rice Prices are Loose and Cheap, and Standard Flour Automatically Moves Downward 115

Yesterday, the flour market showed a downward trend again. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat had rebounded by several points, the overall trend was extremely bad. Because foreign wheat is being purchased gradually, the US side will probably ship the current wheat to China. Moreover, the rice prices are loose and cheap. The autumn harvest is reported to be abundant everywhere. It is difficult to hold back people's hearts. Therefore, although the major factories did not put out large batches in the morning and afternoon, only small factories dumped about 100,000 batches. The rest was returned by longs, and the number was also not small. Observing the subsequent steps, if the major factories continue to put out, or if foreign wheat remains sluggish, it will still be difficult to look high on the market. As a result, the current month fell by 1 fen and 7 li and a half compared to the previous day, November fell by 2 fen and 12 fen, December fell by 2 fen and 2 li and a half, January fell by 2 fen, February fell by 2 fen and 2 li and a half, and March fell by 2 fen and a half.

Wheat Prices Plunge During Peak Season 116

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat market, prices for all months showed a sharp decline. This was due to the gradual weakening of domestic grain prices as a result of abundant harvests and strong reserves. Furthermore, rumors circulated that American wheat loans to China would soon materialize, inevitably dealing a heavy blow to domestic wheat prospects, causing widespread pessimism. The number of sellers gradually increased, as the influx of foreign wheat would naturally lead to the elimination of domestic wheat. As a result, the current month's price fell by four cents compared to the previous week, with November to January falling by six cents each, February falling by eight cents, and March falling by six cents. Spot wheat has already shown signs of weakening. Opening prices were: Yao wheat at 3.52 taels per picul, Yangzhou wheat at 3.37 taels per picul, with a total of 1,300 bags handled by Fuxin and Fufeng companies, it is said.

Reactions from China and Abroad After the Publication of the Lytton Report 124

The Lytton Commission's report, which has attracted global attention, has been published. Public opinion in various countries has also emerged to assess its value. Yesterday, our reporter interviewed leaders from various circles in Shanghai, both Chinese and foreign, to gather their opinions on the League of Nations report. Some thoughtful individuals believe that the report's wording is lengthy and its meaning is quite difficult to grasp, requiring time and careful study to express concrete opinions. Others who do not engage in empty talk emphasize that the Chinese people should strive for self-improvement and actively recover lost territory, believing that the report does not contribute to practical solutions. Wu Chaoshu even stated that the only effective weapon for resolving the Sino-Japanese problem is economic severance. People at the Japanese consulate still believe that the puppet state of Manchukuo cannot be abolished. The following is a summary of opinions from various parties:

▲Wu Chaoshu's Observations

Dr. Wu Chaoshu, a member of the Central Committee, told visitors yesterday that after reading Chapter 7 of the report, he learned that the investigation team was dissatisfied with China's economic severance with Japan. According to Wu's observations, there are two main reasons for this. Based on his numerous experiences attending the League of Nations, he deeply knows that the International Federation has a habit of not daring to offend powerful countries. The Lytton Report stated in the section on the bombing of the South Manchuria Railway that bombing the railway "is not enough to justify the Japanese military action," and also stated that "the Japanese military action that night cannot be regarded as a legitimate defense." It also confirmed that "Manchukuo" was created by Japan. All these delivered major blows to Japan, so it had to use its dissatisfaction with the economic severance as a way to make the powerful and unreasonable Japan feel a little comfortable. This is the first reason. Economic severance, from an international standpoint, can almost be said to have been invented by China. It is also used more in China, but in terms of labor and capital, the act of economic severance was first created by Ireland. The origin of "boycott" is actually an Irish person's name in the past. This person was a large landlord who had a dispute with workers, so the workers devised a way to resist him. Therefore, it has become the commonly used meaning of "resistance" today. When applied internationally, it has become a new weapon invented by China, and European and American countries are quite afraid of it. Therefore, the international community plans to impose sanctions on it. This is the second reason. Wu continued to say that if China now does not even have the weapon of economic severance, then China will definitely not be able to compete in the world. He firmly believes that to solve the Sino-Japanese problem, it is necessary to use diplomatic means to take advantage of the League of Nations and the international situation, as well as military resistance and other methods, but the only effective weapon is economic severance, and this is especially sufficient to show the unity of the Chinese nation. Wu also said that there is no country that has lost its territory that cannot recover it. For example, after the Franco-Prussian War in 1871, France lost the provinces of Alsace and Lorraine to Germany. After more than forty years, France finally recovered its territory in 1919. Poland has been destroyed for hundreds of years, and now it can completely restore its independence and autonomy. The Northeast issue only depends on the extent of the efforts of the people. Wu finally discussed Japan's strength, saying that Japan's military position can be called strong in the Far East, but its navy and army are still inferior to those of the major European and American powers. Although it is difficult for military forces to penetrate deep into the Far East, the economic side is a major weakness of Japan. The English proverb "Heel of Achilles" comes from the classical idiom of ancient Greece. Achilles was a person who, after being born, his father and mother hoped that he would become an immortal. Before long, a god told him that those who could follow him in practice would be able to achieve their wishes. Then the so-called god took his foot and immersed it in the river. All the parts of his body that were wetted by the river water became bronze and iron, and swords could not penetrate it. However, it was not known that the ankles held by the hands were not immersed in water and were still fleshy, and there was this weakness. As a result, Japan's weakness is like this. China's greatest strength is in the economy. To maintain this strength, we must be united and persist to the end, and not rely solely on foreign assistance to be effective.

▲Opinions from the British

A reporter visited Mr. , the chairman of the British Chamber of Commerce. He only took a brief look at the report but felt that the report was very fair. It has two values. First, the various disputes that had previously been based on conflicting claims can now be clarified with this report. Second, China and Japan can obtain a basis for negotiations from this. If China accepts this report and Japan rejects it, China's position in the international community will be more consolidated. The British government and fair people around the world must support this report.

▲Commentary from the Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury

The Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury commented on the report (above omitted). In short, the investigative team’s report cannot be regarded as the conclusion of the Manchurian issue, and that was not its original intention. However, it does provide a summary of the Manchurian incident in a competent and impartial manner, including the organization of the new state, and proposes a feasible solution. There is nothing seriously new proposed. The real problem remains unanswered. This statement is very simple, but the meaning is extremely complex. The question is whether Japan will insist on isolating itself from the world in order to pursue the expansion of its military and political power in the Asian continent without being bound by any other world resolutions. Will people tell Japan what price it is willing to pay up to now that it is willing to pay? Is Japan willing to endanger the German colonies in the Pacific that it manages? This is one of the main parts of the question that it should answer. We

have heard that Japan would rather fight the world than give up Manchuria. This matter is not under discussion for the time being. There is no question of war over Manchuria now. The question today is only whether Japan believes that what it believes is the Manchuria it has obtained and controls is worth the cost of losing its position in the international community.

▲Attitude from the Japanese Side

People at the Japanese consulate stated that they have not yet officially released any opinions on the Lytton Report, but they said that the State of Manchuria has already been produced and cannot be allowed to die prematurely. The only thing to do today is to implement the principle of Europeans ruling Europe, Americans ruling America, and Asians ruling Asia and start all over again. The time for negotiations between China and Japan on the Manchuria issue has passed. Future negotiations will not discuss the Manchuria issue. If China recognizes the current state of affairs and proceeds to negotiate the future relations between China and Japan, Japan will of course do its best.

Wang Jingwei Suffering from Liver Swelling 126

▲Has Telegraphed the Central Executive Committee to Request an Extension of His Leave

▲Chu Minyi Returned to Shanghai with a German Doctor Yesterday

Chu Minyi recently accompanied the German doctor, Dr. Nolbo, by land aircraft from China Aviation to Hangzhou and then to Mogan Mountain to visit Wang Jingwei's illness. Yesterday at 11:50 am, Chu and the German doctor returned to Shanghai by the original plane. Chu immediately went to Qiqi Road at 2:00 pm to visit Song Ziwen to report on Wang's condition, and returned to Beijing by overnight train last night. According to Chu, Wang is suffering from liver swelling and needs to stay in bed for treatment. He has telegraphed Beijing to request an extension of his leave. The following are the recent symptoms of Wang and the original text of the telegram requesting an extension of his leave.

▲Wang's Symptoms

Chu told reporters yesterday: "After we arrived at Mogan Mountain, the German doctor and Mr. Wang conducted a detailed examination three times. According to him, the liver swelling has been slightly reduced, but it is not easy to massage due to excessive gas in the abdomen. Last time, the liver dropped to three fingers' width below the ribs, but now it is only three fingers, which is the result of a week of bed rest. The yellow color of the eyeballs has also faded slightly, and there are still yellow marks on the face. The pulse is slightly slower. Usually it beats eighty times per minute, but now it is sixty-six times. This can also prove that bile enters the blood. The entry of bile into the blood may be due to the liver swelling and the bile ducts being compressed, so this time we took a blood sample and a stool sample back to Shanghai for detailed examination. It is estimated that the blood sample last time contained 0.197% sugar, and the stool sample also contained sugar and bile. The doctor instructed that he still needs to stay in bed in addition to three meals a day, because walking around easily causes the liver to drop. Even when staying in bed, he must lower his pillow and raise the feet of the bed. The diet should avoid foods containing sugar and starch, and now also avoid fat. Therefore, the patient does not find much food palatable. It is estimated that he has lost seven pounds in weight in a week. In terms of treatment, in addition to taking medicine, he also applies a medicinal paste and a hot water bottle to the liver. The doctor said that if the patient can follow this treatment and rest quietly for three weeks, the inflammation of the liver and gallbladder may gradually subside, otherwise he may get chronic hepatitis, and in addition to diabetes, he will have a liver disease.

▲Telegram to the Central Executive Committee

Wang telegraphed the Central Executive Committee on the 2nd to request an extension of his leave, saying: "The Central Executive Committee and the Central Political Conference of the Nanjing government: I am deeply grateful that the Central Committee previously approved my leave of absence for two weeks for recuperation. Now the sugar disease has been slightly reduced, but suddenly liver swelling has been added, and I cannot get out of bed. I have no choice but to ask for an extension of my leave until I recover, when I will return to Beijing to serve. Please take a look. Wang Zhaoming, Winter"

▲Telegram to Chiang Kai-shek

Also telegraphed to Chiang Kai-shek, military committee chairman: "Lushan, Chairman Chiang: I have received your letter. My sugar disease has been reduced, but suddenly liver swelling has been added, and the pain is more severe. The doctor ordered me to stay in bed and first remove the pillow and put the feet of the bed up high, and use medicine inside and outside. In this situation, I cannot but ask the Central Committee for an extension of my leave. I am anxiously concerned and very grateful. Wang Zhaoming, Winter"

Shanghai Municipal Council Orchestra to Broadcast by Radio 131

The Shanghai Municipal Council's orchestra broadcast once via the X.C.B.L. radio station at the beginning of this year. The results were very good, but since the broadcast location required a specially built hall, it was not continued after that. Now the Music Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Council sees that more and more families are installing radios, and plans to hold broadcasts again this winter, once a week. This will be done automatically by the Bureau and will be handled by a certain radio station, but it will not be related to its advertising sequence. Since the radio station provides convenience and does not charge a fee, the Bureau will charge the broadcasting company that hires the orchestra according to the example of hiring the entire team or a part of it for a reduction of two tenths, and it will also allow it to calculate each time for at least half an hour (usually at least one hour), but it should not affect long-term performances elsewhere. It is planned to start this broadcast this winter and hold it every Thursday afternoon from 9:00 to 10:15. The Board of Directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council has already approved this plan. From now on, the performance of the orchestra will be more popular among the general audience.

Regarding Discussions on Commercial Lawsuits 132

Yesterday, a reporter visited an employee of the Commercial Press regarding the case of dismissed employees suing the company's board of directors in court, demanding retirement pensions and severance bonuses. The following is a record of the conversation:

(1) Retirement Pension: It is said that the company indeed had a compensation regulation before the January 28th Incident. Employees who were dismissed would be given a certain amount of retirement pay, the amount depending on the length of their service and the amount of their salary. However, this regulation only applied to normal times and could not be applied after extraordinary changes. Furthermore, the rights to interpret and amend it belonged to the company's board of directors. The compensation was paid from the company's surplus, with the annual allocation and accumulated amount over the years serving as a compensation fund to cover all expenses under the aforementioned regulations. However, the regulations stated that this fund still belonged to the company. In May of this year, the company received approval from the Social Affairs Bureau to allocate the remaining fund entirely to the dismissed employees as a final relief measure. The company made great efforts to comply, and the fund has now been exhausted.

(2) Severance Pay: In addition to the retirement pension under the aforementioned compensation regulations, the company has no other agreement to provide severance pay to employees. The precedent cited by the plaintiffs, the China Eastern Manufacturing Factory, was that when China Eastern closed down, the company's business was thriving. Out of sympathy for some of the dismissed employees, they were given some extra salary, but this was a special donation and could not be used as a precedent, let alone applied to the deeply painful situation today. Moreover, after the China Eastern incident, the company dismissed many employees, but there was never a case of extra salary being given like in the China Eastern case, which can serve as clear proof. As for this time, when the company dismissed employees, each person was given about two months' salary, but this was all done voluntarily by the company and there is no reason to use it as a basis for litigation.

(3) Bonuses: The company's financial settlement for the previous year was extended to the end of January this year because when the war broke out, it was during the company's inventory time, and all goods and books were completely destroyed. Even if the company had a surplus, it had completely turned into a loss by the time of settlement. Moreover, the company's regulations stipulate that bonuses can only be distributed to employees when shareholders have dividends. Now that a large part of the company's assets has been destroyed and shareholders' equity has been reduced by two-fifths, there are no bonuses to speak of.

Finally, the reporter asked whether the company had ten million yuan of war risk insurance in Hong Kong. The person smiled and replied that if the company had war risk insurance, how could the shareholders have suffered a reduction in equity? Anyone with a little knowledge can tell that this is undeniable and there is no need to argue.

Unable to Marry, He Committed Suicide by Hanging 137

▲ Zhang Yuping, a Pitiable Case

Zhang Yuping, from Gaoyou, Jiangbei, is twenty-five years old this year and has not yet married. He is currently working as a water boiler at the Xingfa Garden teahouse, opened by his elder brother Zhang Yuqi, at 298 Rue Lartigue in the French Concession, earning a meager monthly salary. Yesterday, they reported to the Second Special Court, and Prosecutor Deng Baosun came to the hall to examine the body. According to the complaint from the deceased's brother and witnesses, the official ruled that Zhang Yuping committed suicide by hanging himself and authorized his brother Zhang Yuqi to collect the body for burial after signing a guarantee.

Flour Sacks Filled with Gunpowder 138

▲ Taken from Artillery Shells

▲ Both Defendants Fined 100 Yuan Each

Around 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, Chinese detective Shen Yuzhou from the Yangshupu Police Station discovered that two men from Hubei, Yang Huaxing and Yang Shunxing, were carrying two sacks of flour at the Tengyue Road Wharf. They hired a sampan, planning to go to the Changjiang Steamer, acting flustered and suspicious. The detective stepped forward to question them, but they gave evasive answers. Upon opening the sacks, they were found to be filled with about seventy pounds of gunpowder. They were taken to the police station and, yesterday morning, escorted to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Fu Lin presided over the criminal court. The police station's lawyer presented the case, stating that the two defendants claimed in the police station that the gunpowder was purchased from a scrap metal shop in Nanshi in August of this year and that they intended to take it back to their hometown in Hubei for use by the local security team. However, they could not provide a passport upon request, which was clearly a false statement. The gunpowder was different from ordinary gunpowder. The police station's investigation revealed that it was taken from artillery shells. In previous similar cases involving the disposal of such explosive materials, the materials were confiscated and stored in the stolen goods warehouse, which was considered dangerous. It was requested that the materials be handed over to the police station for destruction. When questioned, the defendants admitted that they were taking it back to their hometown for use by the defense regiment. After verifying the confession, Judge Fu sentenced the defendants to a fine of one hundred yuan each for the crime of possessing explosive materials. If they were unable to pay the fine, it would be commuted to one day of imprisonment for every three yuan. The gunpowder was handed over to the police station for disposal.

Apprentice at Money Exchange Runs Off with Three Thousand Yuan 139

▲ Eloping with a Prostitute to Fulfill Their Dreams

▲ The Stolen Money Found Under the Pillow

▲ Only Five Dollars Spent

▲ Sentenced to Three Months in Prison, Sentence Suspended

Zhang Mengzhou, a native of Ningbo, is seventeen years old and has been working as an apprentice at the Hongsheng Money Exchange at 230 Sichuan Road for two years. He is usually very careful and conscientious in his work, so he is highly trusted by manager Xu Chengzhi. On the morning of the first of this month, at 10:15 AM, Xu Chengzhi ordered Zhang and the other two apprentices, Qi Weiran and Luo Xueyong, to go to the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank at No. 7 The Bund to withdraw 18,000 yuan. Luo hid 11,000 yuan, Qi hid 4,000 yuan, and Zhang carried 3,000 yuan. On the way back to the exchange, when they reached the intersection of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, Zhang suddenly disappeared. After searching everywhere without success, Xu Chengzhi reported the incident to the General Police Station and requested an investigation. Later, the exchange received a phone call from a Mr. Xia, who stated that Zhang had left a leather suitcase at his place and that someone was coming to pick it up. Xia suspected something was amiss, so he called to ask if Zhang had sent the person. After the exchange confirmed Xia's address, they ordered detective Jiang Shangpei to go to Mr. Xia's residence at No. 35 Beishan Road to retrieve Zhang's suitcase. The police found a photo of a woman in the suitcase. Detective Jiang conducted a detailed investigation and learned that the woman, named Wang Lanhua, was from Yixing, seventeen years old, and worked as a prostitute at No. 8 Lane, Rue Amiral Bayle in the French Concession. She had been in a relationship with Zhang for three months and had become intimate. The detective secretly went to the brothel at 11:00 PM the night before and found Zhang inside, fast asleep with Wang. He woke them up and found the original banknotes, 2,995 yuan, hidden under the pillow, only five yuan short, which he had already spent. He immediately took them to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special Court's Criminal Court. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated the case and requested that he be prosecuted for embezzlement in the course of business under Article 357 of the Criminal Law. Xu Chengzhi then explained the circumstances of sending them to withdraw the money and stated that the defendant's conduct had always been quite good and that this was his first offense, so he did not want to pursue the matter further and requested a suspended sentence. When questioned, the defendant admitted that he had committed the crime due to temporary confusion and requested leniency. Qian Hongye, the head of the Criminal Court, verified the confession and announced the verdict in court: Zhang Mengzhou was sentenced to six months in prison for the crime of embezzling objects held in the course of business, with a three-year suspended sentence. The stolen money was returned to the plaintiff.

▲ Discovered by Her Husband for Her Immoral Behavior

▲ Deeply Regretful, She Had a Thought of World-Weariness

Duan Yi, a woman from Hubei, was twenty-three years old. Her husband, Duan Henghe, was a barber. Li Quansheng Hanged Himself on the Drying Terrace 142

▲ Annoyed for Failing to Borrow Money from His Mistress

On the evening of the 1st of this month, a local named Li Quansheng went to the beancurd shop opened by his friend Lu Gensheng at 406 Route Tenant de la Tour to look for his mistress, Shao Wu, and ask for money. Frustrated by not getting it, he suddenly had a thought of world-weariness and secretly went to the shop's drying terrace, where he hanged himself from the railing with his belt. The next morning, Fei Amao, a neighbor in the shop, caught a glimpse of him and immediately notified Lu Gensheng and others, who untied him, but he had already died of asphyxiation. They reported the incident to the Huizi Police Station, which sent detectives to investigate and took the body to the morgue on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, they reported to the First Special District Local Court, which commissioned Inspector Zhan Liangce to come to the morgue to examine the body. According to Fei Amao, who is twenty-four years old, he went to the drying terrace at 6:00 AM that morning and caught a glimpse of the deceased hanging from the drying terrace next door. He immediately notified and helped untie him. Lu Gensheng stated that he rented a three-story beancurd shop. Shao Wu was a friend of his wife and often came to his place to chat. On that day, Wu came first, and Li Quansheng came later to ask her for money. When she refused, Li left the room. He did not know that he had hanged himself on the drying terrace. Shao Wu stated that she was thirty-nine years old, a local resident living in Huaxingfang, and had no adulterous relationship with the deceased. She only knew him because he was a tailor who made her clothes, so she recognized him. However, he often borrowed money from her, and she gave him some relief because she saw that he was poor. He borrowed money from her again that day, and she replied that she could lend him a few dollars tomorrow. She saw him leave the room and then went to bed at Lu's place, not knowing that he had suddenly hanged himself. After verifying the confessions, Zhan Jun ruled that the deceased Li Quansheng had indeed committed suicide by hanging himself. There was no family of the deceased, so the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.

It is also heard that all goods will be uniformly discounted and then further discounted, making the goods high in quality and low in price, which is truly a rare opportunity in the midst of price reductions.

Painters are often divided into the Shanghai School and the Northern School. Generally, the Shanghai School emphasizes vividness, while the Northern School emphasizes structure. He learned in the South and was refined in the North, and can be said to be the mainstay of contemporary artists. Crabs and Pomegranates Should Never Be Eaten Together 166

▲ New Homicide in Nanjing

▲ Attention to Those Who Enjoy Holding Crabs and Devouring Them

As the autumn wind blows fiercely, fat crabs appear on the market, perfect for enjoying with wine. The joy of holding a crab and devouring it is an endless pleasure that people recognize in this world. We only know that crabs and persimmons are mutually antagonistic and should not be eaten together. Who knows that eating crabs with pomegranates can also lead to death? Here is a record of a strange homicide case from Xiaguan, Nanjing, where someone ate pomegranates and crabs together. A villager came to the city to buy goods for his son's upcoming wedding. He attended a banquet at a friend's house in Xiaguan. The friend knew that he was fond of drinking and that fresh crabs were on the market, so he cooked crabs to accompany the wine. The villager was very enthusiastic, devouring and drinking heartily until he was completely drunk. After getting drunk, he felt a burning sensation and was unbearably thirsty, so he bought several pomegranates and ate them all ravenously. A moment later, he suddenly had severe abdominal pain and felt extremely ill, repeatedly shouting "I'm uncomfortable!" and "Help!" After about one or two hours, he suddenly died. According to the doctor, the villager suffered from crab poisoning. Eating pomegranates and crabs together is dangerously lethal, but he died ignorantly, which is truly tragic. Those who love to eat crabs should be aware of this warning.

▲ Seventh Time

The Shanghai Office of the Soochow Province War Zone Relief Committee held its seventh office meeting the day before yesterday. According to Commissioner Jiang Wenyu's relay of Director Shu's report, the provincial funds were insufficient, and the promised 10,000 yuan for the relief of elementary schools would still need to be divided into three installments. Municipal Land Bureau Announces That Owners Should Submit Evidence to the Bureau 168

▲ Ministry Certificate, Imperial Edict, and Receipt Tickets

▲ Submit All Within Six Months

The Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau issued an announcement yesterday stating that the bureau is organizing land and issuing land practice certificates as the only proof of ownership of real estate. Each certificate is accompanied by a topographic map, detailing the location of the household land, the four boundaries, and the length dimensions of the owner's area. All old field deeds, division deeds, agency deeds, imperial edicts, and other documents will be taken back and invalidated, and land certificates will be issued in exchange. As the project is nearing completion, announcements have been made in stages for the exchange of certificates. It has been found that the Ministry Certificates that have been assessed for grain and the County Certificates and Imperial Edicts issued by the county that are not recorded in the old printed records are generally inconsistent. Moreover, there are no property acres, or it is not known where the land is located. In order to organize this land and protect the property rights of owners, the Bureau specifically issues this announcement urging all owners to promptly submit the Ministry Certificates or County Certificates Imperial Edicts that have been assessed for grain and the receipt tickets for grain paid over the years within six months from the date of this announcement, so that the Bureau can verify the measurement and exchange them for land practice certificates to manage the property. This matter concerns property rights, so please do not delay or harm yourselves. This is hereby announced.

Rice Milling Industry Association Resolves to Restrict Mortgage Methods 170

At yesterday's executive committee meeting of the Shanghai Rice Milling Industry Association, Chairman Zhang Nianju reported the purpose of the meeting, which was that the mortgaged amount of cargo transported to Shanghai exceeded the price of the goods. The milling agents were unable to repay the mortgaged amount, harming the industry. A remedy should be discussed. After discussion, it was unanimously agreed that the Anhui and Ningbo rice transported to Shanghai were mortgaged to various banks and money shops in Xiaguan by the transport companies acting as agents. The mortgaged amount often exceeded the price of the goods. If the market price fell, the shippers would often avoid coming to Shanghai due to losses, which had frequently harmed the industry over the years. It was decided to use 200 pounds of coarse indica rice as the standard for the current market price, and the mortgage amount, including freight, should not exceed five yuan. If the packaged amount is large, the same principle will be applied. Future market price increases or decreases will be reported to the industry at any time. If any excessive mortgage is approved privately, the milling will be punished by public discussion once it is verified. A letter will be sent to the financial institutions in Xiaguan that specialize in mortgages and the Transportation Association, requesting that they inform the transportation companies to pay attention to the handling. An announcement will be published to inform the cargo shippers. The meeting was adjourned after discussing other cases.

Tianzhang Paper Mill Labor Dispute Resolved 171

▲ General Wage Increase of Five Cents Per Person

▲ Implemented from the Sixteenth of This Month

The New Sound Society reported that the workers of the Tianzhang Paper Mill demanded improved treatment, which led to a strike. Although the government advised them to resume work first, the wage dispute was mediated by Party and government agencies. It has now been two months. At 2:00 PM yesterday, the Bureau of Social Affairs convened the Labor-Capital Mediation Committee for a final mediation. Labor representatives Wu Gensheng and Yang Guanhua, and capital representatives Liu Yuanshi and Di Zhaolin, attended. The chairman, mediator Zhu Guilin, first reported the mediation process, followed by separate statements from the labor and capital sides. After a long period of discussion, the two sides finally agreed and signed the minutes as follows: The dispute between the parties is over wages. The committee convened a mediation, and now the agreement signed by both parties is specially recorded as follows: (1) All workers directly paid wages by the factory will receive a general wage increase of five cents per day. However, workers whose wages have been automatically increased by the factory by more than five cents this year and newly hired workers this year are exempt from the increase. (2) The date of the above wage increase will be implemented from October 16th of this year. This matter has been signed and mediated with the consent of representatives of both parties, and should be regarded as a labor agreement between the parties in dispute.

Opium Found on Beijing-Shanghai Train 173

▲ Garrison Command Requests the Railway Bureau to Hand Over People

The Songhu Garrison Command's Detective Team received a tip-off the day before yesterday stating that someone was secretly transporting a large number of contraband items, etc., and entrusted the Beijing-Shanghai train driver to secretly transport them to Shanghai. Bureau of Social Affairs, etc., Re-investigates War Zone Damage Statistics 174

▲ Urges War Zone Residents to Register Damage as Soon as Possible

After the Shanghai War, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Accountants Association jointly sent personnel to investigate the approximate amount of damage in the war zone. They first published a rough estimate of the damage in April and May of this year. It is expected to be finalized within this month. However, because the investigation of the three agencies is entirely based on the reports of war zone victims, and there are many victims who have not reported, reaching nearly half, this report cannot be said to be completely complete.

The Four Criminals Apprehended in the Settlement 175

▲ Identified by Wu Guangzong's Family

The National News Agency reports that Wu Guangzong, director of the Hydrographic Office of the Naval Department, was shot dead by thugs at his private residence in Ningkang Lane, Anlan Road, Ximen, on the morning of September 21st. The Municipal Government of Shanghai immediately ordered the Municipal Police Department to instruct Lu Ying, the captain of the detective team, and Jin Tian, the district chief of the second district, to solve the case within three days, strictly apprehend the criminals, and bring them to justice. Details were reported in a previous publication.

It is now known that the case has been solved by Lu Ying, the captain of the municipal detective team. The bandits were hiding in the Dahua Hotel on Fuzhou Road and the Juelu Hotel on Xizang Road. Personnel were immediately dispatched to request the Zhabei Police Department to send additional Chinese and foreign officers to arrest four suspects at the addresses last night. Four pistols and thirty-four bullets were seized, and the words "Shanghai Municipal Police Department" were engraved on the magazines and barrels. All were immediately detained at the police station. The detectives, together with Chinese officers from the relevant police district, drove to Wu's residence in Ningkang Lane and summoned Shen Taihua, the bodyguard, Chen Yongkuan, the male servant, and Qiu Ren, the female servant, to the police station for identification. Four random prisoners of mixed ethnicity were deliberately placed among the four arrested suspects. After Xu Taihua and others separately identified the group, three of the suspects were identified as the ones who held guns and assassinated Wu at his home. The police department then transferred them to the Special First Court for preliminary interrogation before returning them to custody.

At 10:00 AM the following morning, Lu Ying, the captain of the Municipal Police Department's detective team, personally led Gu Liancheng, the team leader, and six other detectives to the police station to request the police chief to temporarily transfer the suspects to the detective team for questioning. The police chief agreed to bring them over, but stated that they would be returned to the police station for detention at 4:00 PM that afternoon.

During the interrogation, the four suspects confessed as follows:

One identified himself as Song Jiande, from Henan, 30 years old. He came to Shanghai from his hometown on September 2nd and met a colleague, Mr. Jia, who is currently a detective in the Second Regiment of the Huzhou Security Office. Mr. Jia invited him to stay at the Dahua Hotel on Fuzhou Road and told him to go to the Chinese district at 7:00 AM on the 21st to handle some business.

Another identified himself as Zhang Shaoliang, from Henan, 23 years old, residing on the third floor of the Dahua Hotel. He came to Shanghai from Henan on September 16th to look for his old superior, Zhu Jieren's adjutant, but was unsuccessful. He had dinner at a certain restaurant and ran into some fellow villagers who asked him why he had come to Shanghai. He replied that he was looking for a friend and had not found him. They invited him to work in Huzhou on a case and immediately sent him to the Dahua Hotel. At 7:00 AM on September 21st, they asked him what kind of gun he could use, and then gave him a six-inch Browning pistol. He and Song Jiande and two others each held pistols and went to a certain lane of unknown location. They told him to guard the back door while they went inside, went upstairs, and fired shots. They then fled back to the hotel together.

Another, Wu Jize, from Henan, 24 years old, residing in Hongxing, Huzhou. On August 9th, he met a fellow villager, Mr. Jia, a detective in the Second Regiment of the Huzhou Security Office, in front of the Dahua Hotel. Mr. Jia called him inside and asked him to help handle the case, claiming it was an official matter. He stayed for two days. On the morning of September 21st, he was given a pistol and told to go to the Chinese district to handle the case. It was true that the detective knocked on the door and went inside to assassinate Wu.

The suspect Yao Jiechen confessed that he was from Huzhou, 38 years old, a farmer living in a certain village near Hongxing Bridge in Changxing. He came to Shanghai a day ago to find work for his son and stayed at Chen Xuejiang's home in Jixiang Lane, Zhoushan Road. Because the house was being demolished and rebuilt, he was planning to return home when he heard that Li Lianyuan, the detective chief of the Second Regiment of the Huzhou Security Office, had been arrested for an incident. He went to the Dahua Hotel to inquire and met an absconding suspect, Mr. Jia, who borrowed more than twenty yuan from him to pay for the room fee, promising to return it in two or three days. So he went to collect the debt that day and was detained.

Fire Insurance Representatives from Disaster Area Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 177

▲ Also Seeking Compensation from Sincere Company

The Shanghai Fire Insurance Compensation Coordination Committee for the disaster area held an emergency meeting the day before yesterday and decided to petition the insurance companies yesterday for compensation. Prior to this, they had consulted with the Third District Party Headquarters to use the Tianhou Palace Bridge as a gathering place and notified all policyholders to gather there. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, approximately 500 people arrived on time. Around 9:00 AM, they formed a procession and first went to Sincere Company to demand compensation, led by the chief commander, Wang Zhixiang. Wang Zhixiang, Hu Yibo, Situ Ji, Ma Juegen, and others were selected to negotiate with the company. The others waited on the side of the road. Liang Guohua, the manager of the company, met with the representatives. Liang said that he would be responsible for compensation within the scope, but excessive demands were difficult to accept. The Public Works Department considered that the gathering was disrupting traffic and ordered the police to disperse the crowd. Around 12:00 noon, the policyholders returned to Tianhou Palace, but Shuji Elementary School in Tianhou Palace notified the Fifth District Police Station to resolve the disturbance caused by the large crowd. The Fifth District Police Station immediately dispatched a patrol officer and eight policemen to Tianhou Palace to persuade the crowd to disperse. The residents elected Wang Zhixiang, Liang Guohua, and eight other representatives to petition the Municipal Government. Approximately thirty residents volunteered to follow. They arrived at the Municipal Government around 3:00 PM. The representatives submitted their cards requesting to see the mayor, while those who followed waited quietly outside the gate for a reply. Mayor Wu sent Director Yuan Shenglu to meet with them. Yuan expressed his views on the various requests made by the representatives, stating that the Municipal Government sympathized with the suffering of the disaster-stricken citizens and hoped to find good solutions for relief. However, all solutions could not deviate from the law or ignore the facts. Therefore, the Municipal Government was unwilling to make empty promises that would be difficult to implement. He would convey the opinions of the representatives to the mayor to carefully consider a solution that balanced both law and fact. As for designating a location for gatherings, it was best to contact the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The Municipal Government would provide legal protection. The representatives were immediately satisfied and left.

Further Demands for Compensation Today: The association stated that yesterday's contact with the company yielded no results, and the Municipal Government was also unable to provide concrete solutions. However, the disaster-stricken households were in dire straits and would take effective measures. Without sacrifice, there would be no success. Tomorrow (today) they would continue to expand publicity and demonstrations.

Mrs. Moll has close ties with Senator Borah, chairman of the Foreign Relations Committee of the U.S. Senate. Major American newspapers have hired her to go to Germany to investigate the development of German politics. According to a letter from Counselor Liang of our embassy in Germany yesterday, Mrs. Moll left Hamburg on August 22nd aboard the Danish ship Adrica via Suez and will arrive in Shanghai on the 7th of this month.

Record of the Fourth Day of the Chinese Medical Association Conference 179

The Chinese Medical Association continued its conference yesterday. At 9:00 AM, a business meeting was held. The first topic discussed was the journal issue. The members present believed that original papers should be fully published because the association's journal had a wide circulation not only in China but also had a large number of foreign subscribers. If it could be improved with greater effort and rigorous review, it would certainly attract the attention of the international medical community. It was regrettable that the cost of reprints of articles in the journal was too high and should be reduced to increase circulation. The meeting then discussed the association's charter. After revisions by Dr. Liu Ruiheng and Dr. Jin Baoshan, with input from Dr. Song Wusheng, Dr. Zhu Hengbi, Dr. Chen Wanli, and Dr. Yan Fuqing, it was agreed that the charter should be simple and the detailed rules should be detailed. The general assembly then voted to have the executive committee revise the association's charter without submitting it to the general assembly again for approval.

After the business meeting, a general meeting of the Department of Internal Medicine was held. The program included Pumay's "Problems of Lung Disease in China," Chang Sun's "Neurological Diseases Discovered in Yunnan," Zhu Shenzhi's "Application of Douzhi Feeding for Infants," Kantaber's "Epidemic Meningitis," and Luo Aisi's "Skin Diseases." More than 200 people attended.

After lunch, group meetings were held in the departments of Internal Medicine, Surgery, Public Health, Pathology, and Physiology. At 3:00 PM, the General Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society specially provided multiple cars to take the members to visit the new site of the National Shanghai Medical College. The college is located to the left of the General Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society on Haig Road. The new building consists of two four-story buildings. The first building houses the library, offices, and student dormitories, and the second building houses the classrooms and research rooms of the pre-medical and basic science departments. After the visit, they went to the hospital to visit the clinical departments, outpatient clinics, and wards. After a tour, at 4:00 PM, President Yan and other staff members hosted tea and refreshments on the lawn. Another group was taken by the Public Works Department in cars from the Lister Institute to visit the department's slaughterhouse. At 7:00 PM, the members went to the Zhimeilou Restaurant on Fuzhou Road for a banquet hosted by the Shanghai Branch. Toasts were exchanged, and guests and hosts enjoyed themselves.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Ends Cholera Prevention Work 180

▲ A Total of 786,407 Injections Administered

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau has always made great efforts to prevent cholera during the summer and autumn seasons each year. Since 1927, the harm caused by cholera in Shanghai has been greatly reduced. This year, due to the aftermath of the war and the discovery of patients with true cholera in late April, the bureau took the prevention work more seriously than in previous years, implementing disinfection and free vaccination, and promoting knowledge of epidemic prevention. Free vaccinations have been carried out since May 1st. Now that the weather is cooling in autumn and no cholera cases have been found, the prevention work was officially ended at the end of September. A total of 786,407 injections were administered this year, an increase of more than 200,000 injections compared to last year. Therefore, although the cholera outbreak this year was fierce, it did not become a major disaster due to the early implementation of various preventive measures.
